Using new builder (from HEAD), auto-build off.

In a self-hosting workspace, I was trying to reproduce a bug in a project 
named 'Crap'. I happen to have source projects for 'org.eclipse.jdt.core' 
and 'org.eclipse.jdt.ui'.

Also 'Crap' happens to refer to 'org.eclipse.jdt.core' on its classpath.

1. I did first a full build of all projects.
2. In 'Crap''s default package, I defined a type named 'Amb' using the following
   content:

[import java.sql.Date;
import java.util.Date;


public class Amb {

}]

3. I request an incremental build (ctrl-B), and noticed it was heavily 
recompiling 'org.eclipse.jdt.ui' for no apparent reason.

Here is the tracing info (workspace available upon request):

In a self-hosting workspace, I was trying to reproduce a bug in a project 
named 'Crap'. I happen to have source projects for 'org.eclipse.jdt.core' 
and 'org.eclipse.jdt.ui'.

Also 'Crap' happens to refer to 'org.eclipse.jdt.core' on its classpath.

1. I did first a full build of all projects.
2. In 'Crap''s default package, I defined a type named 'Amb' using the following
   content:

[import java.sql.Date;
import java.util.Date;


public class Amb {

}]

3. I request an incremental build (ctrl-B), and noticed it was heavily 
recompiling 'org.eclipse.jdt.ui' for no apparent reason.

*********************************************************************
From the trace its clear that org.eclipse.jdt.core was rebuilt fully but 
org.eclipse.jdt.ui was not. When an incremental build was requested, all the 
class files in org.eclipse.jdt.core appeared changed to org.eclipse.jdt.ui.

Do you have the trace for the last build of org.eclipse.jdt.core?
After a phone conversation, we figured out that the problem was caused by the 
Project references for org.eclipse.jdt.ui NOT being set. So it was built before 
org.eclipse.jdt.core and did not see all of the class file changes until its 
next build.
Actually, project references not being set is a bug of JDTCORE.
Support for updating references is in, but on the #setRawClasspath path, it 
does not seem to be involved (though it does on other pathes).

Entering proper Bug for it.
